- 4vCPU, 8GM RAM, GPU with 10~16 GB VRAM
- 5 replicas

# Solution - Kelpie JQ + self-managed data sync (upload thread and queue, rclone and Cloudflare R2)

# Jobs - 5 jobs with each running 48 hours (for loop only)
